				<p>Cheap Car Auto Insurance Quotes Explained in Simple Terms Car auto insurance quotes are price estimates given by insurance companies that show how much you may pay for car insurance coverage. These quotes are calculated using details such as your driving history, vehicle information, location, and coverage preferences.
